OBJECT Report 51105 Import Loc. 9 (GS) Files
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=07/01/20;
    Time=12:00:00 AM;
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=ENU=Import Loc. 9 (GS) Files;
    OnInitReport=BEGIN
                   LocationCode := '9';
                 END;

    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  WhseReleaseLine.LOCKTABLE;
                  WhseReleaseLine.DELETEALL;
                END;

    OnPostReport=BEGIN
                   WhseReleaseLine.DELETEALL;
                 END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1000000000;;DataItem;xFile             ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000022;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Path,Is a file,Name)
                                 WHERE(Path=CONST(U:\WAREHOUSE FILES\GSNG\),
                                       Is a file=CONST(Yes));
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  CommonInpFile.TEXTMODE(FALSE);
                                  CommonInpFile.OPEN(xFile.Path + xFile.Name);

                                  TempDocLine := '';

                                  i := 0;
                                  j := 0;

                                  REPEAT
                                    IF CommonInpFile.READ(Char) = 0 THEN
                                      j := 1;
                                    IF (Char = 10) OR (Char = 13) THEN BEGIN
                                      WriteOK := TRUE;
                                      Char := 0;
                                    END;
                                    i := i + 1;
                                    TempDocLine[i] := Char;
                                    IF WriteOK OR (i = 80) THEN BEGIN
                                      CodeString := COPYSTR(TempDocLine,1,4);
                                      CodeLineNo := COPYSTR(TempDocLine,5,6);
                                      CASE CodeString OF
                                        '0000':
                                          BEGIN
                                            ReleaseNo := 0;
                                            EVALUATE(BatchDate,COPYSTR(TempDocLine,11,6));
                                            EVALUATE(BatchTime,COPYSTR(TempDocLine,17,4));
                                          END;
                                        '0200': ;
                                        '0201':
                                          BEGIN
                                            ReleaseNo := 0;
                                            EVALUATE(ReleaseNo,COPYSTR(TempDocLine,11,6));
                                            CustNo := ClearTailSpace(COPYSTR(TempDocLine,46,5));
                                            EVALUATE(OrderDate,COPYSTR(TempDocLine,71,6));
                                          END;
                                        '0202':
                                          BEGIN
                                            ExternalDocumentNo := ClearTailSpace(COPYSTR(TempDocLine,29,20));
                                            ShippingAgentAndService := ClearTailSpace(COPYSTR(TempDocLine,58,20));
                                          END;
                                        '0203':
                                          BEGIN
                                            ShippingPaymentType := ClearTailSpace(COPYSTR(TempDocLine,69,20));
                                          END;
                                        '0204': ;
                                        '0205':
                                          BEGIN
                                            EVALUATE(BackorderNo,COPYSTR(TempDocLine,11,6));
                                            IF BackorderNo <> ReleaseNo THEN
                                              ReleaseNo := BackorderNo;

                                            EVALUATE(ShipmentDate,COPYSTR(TempDocLine,20,6));
                                            EVALUATE(FreightChargeAmt,COPYSTR(TempDocLine,26,8));

                                            SalesHeader.INIT;
                                            SalesHeader.SetHideValidationDialog(TRUE);
                                            SalesHeader."Document Type" := SalesHeader."Document Type"::Order;
                                            SalesHeader."No." := '';
                                            SalesHeader.INSERT(TRUE);
                                            SalesHeader."Warehouse Release No." := FORMAT(ReleaseNo);
                                            IF Cust.GET(CustNo) THEN
                                              SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Sell-to Customer No.",CustNo)
                                            ELSE
                                              SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Sell-to Customer No.",'00000');
                                            SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Shortcut Dimension 5 Code",'E');
                                            SalesHeader."Document Date" := BatchDate;
                                            SalesHeader."Order Date" := OrderDate;
                                            SalesHeader."Shipment Date" := ShipmentDate;
                                            // <TPZHOTFIX>
                                            SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Location Code",LocationCode);
                                            // </TPZHOTFIX>
                                            SalesHeader."External Document No." := ExternalDocumentNo;

                                            IF LocSASMpng.GET(LocationCode,ShippingAgentAndService) THEN BEGIN
                                              SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Shipping Agent Code",LocSASMpng."Shipping Agent Code");
                                              SalesHeader.VALIDATE("E-Ship Agent Service",LocSASMpng."E-Ship Agent Service");
                                            END ELSE BEGIN
                                              IF STRPOS(ShippingAgentAndService,'UPS') <> 0 THEN
                                                SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Shipping Agent Code",'UPS');

                                              IF ShippingAgent.GET(COPYSTR(ShippingAgentAndService,1,10)) THEN
                                                SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Shipping Agent Code",COPYSTR(ShippingAgentAndService,1,10));

                                              IF ShippingAgentAndService = 'PICK UP' THEN
                                                SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Shipping Agent Code",'PICKUP');
                                            END;
                                          END;
                                        '0211': ;
                                        '0212': ;
                                        '0221':
                                          BEGIN
                                            EVALUATE(SalesHeader."Ship-to Name",ClearTailSpace(COPYSTR(TempDocLine,11,30)));
                                            EVALUATE(SalesHeader."Ship-to Address",ClearTailSpace(COPYSTR(TempDocLine,41,30)));
                                          END;
                                        '0222':
                                          BEGIN
                                            EVALUATE(SalesHeader."Ship-to Address 2",ClearTailSpace(COPYSTR(TempDocLine,11,30)));
                                            EVALUATE(SalesHeader."Ship-to City",ClearTailSpace(COPYSTR(TempDocLine,41,20)));
                                            EVALUATE(SalesHeader."Ship-to County",ClearTailSpace(COPYSTR(TempDocLine,61,2)));
                                            EVALUATE(SalesHeader."Ship-to Post Code",ClearTailSpace(COPYSTR(TempDocLine,63,10)));

                                            IF (SalesHeader."Ship-to Address" = '') OR
                                               (SalesHeader."Ship-to Address" = ' ')
                                            THEN BEGIN
                                              SalesHeader."Ship-to Address" := SalesHeader."Ship-to Address 2";
                                              SalesHeader."Ship-to Address 2" := '';
                                            END;

                                            SalesHeader.MODIFY(TRUE);
                                          END;
                                        '0231': ;
                                        '0232':
                                          BEGIN
                                            EVALUATE(Comment,ClearTailSpace(COPYSTR(TempDocLine,14,80)));
                                            IF Comment <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                              SalesCommentLine.RESET;
                                              SalesCommentLine.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesCommentLine."Document Type"::Order);
                                              SalesCommentLine.SETRANGE("No.",SalesHeader."No.");
                                              SalesCommentLine.SETRANGE("Document Line No.",0);
                                              IF SalesCommentLine.FINDLAST THEN
                                                CommentLineNo := SalesCommentLine."Line No." + 10000
                                              ELSE
                                                CommentLineNo := 10000;

                                              SalesCommentLine.INIT;
                                              SalesCommentLine."Document Type" := SalesCommentLine."Document Type"::Order;
                                              SalesCommentLine."No." := SalesHeader."No.";
                                              SalesCommentLine."Line No." := CommentLineNo;
                                              SalesCommentLine.Comment := Comment;
                                              SalesCommentLine.INSERT;

                                              WhseReleaseLine.RESET;
                                              WhseReleaseLine.SETRANGE("Location Code",SalesHeader."Location Code");
                                              WhseReleaseLine.SETRANGE("File Name",xFile.Name);
                                              WhseReleaseLine.SETRANGE("Release No.",ReleaseNo);

                                              IF (STRPOS(ShippingAgentAndService,'UPS') <> 0) AND
                                                 (COPYSTR(Comment,1,2) = '1Z')
                                              THEN BEGIN
                                                //<TPZ1346>
                                                //SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Package Tracking No.",Comment);
                                                SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Package Tracking No.",COPYSTR(Comment, 1, 18));
                                                //</TPZ1346>
                                                SalesHeader.MODIFY;
                                              END;

                                              TrackingNoIndicatorPos := STRPOS(Comment,'#');
                                              //<TPZ1346>
                                              //IF TrackingNoIndicatorPos <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                              IF (TrackingNoIndicatorPos <> 0) AND (SalesHeader."Package Tracking No." = '') THEN BEGIN
                                              //</TPZ1346>
                                                SalesHeader.VALIDATE(
                                                  "Package Tracking No.",
                                                  Trim(COPYSTR(Comment,TrackingNoIndicatorPos + 1,MAXSTRLEN(SalesHeader."Package Tracking No."))));
                                                SalesHeader.MODIFY;
                                              END;
                                            END;
                                          END;
                                        '0251':
                                          BEGIN
                                            SalesLine2.RESET;
                                            SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHeader."Document Type");
                                            SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesHeader."No.");
                                            IF SalesLine2.FINDLAST THEN
                                              LineNo := SalesLine2."Line No." + 10000
                                            ELSE
                                              LineNo := 10000;

                                            SalesLine.INIT;
                                            SalesLine."Document Type" := SalesHeader."Document Type";
                                            SalesLine."Document No." := SalesHeader."No.";
                                            SalesLine."Line No." := LineNo;
                                            SalesLine.INSERT(TRUE);
                                            SalesLine."Sell-to Customer No." := SalesHeader."Sell-to Customer No.";
                                            SalesLine.Type := SalesLine.Type::Item;

                                            EVALUATE(ItemNo,ClearTailSpace(COPYSTR(TempDocLine,15,15)));
                                            IF NOT Item.GET(ItemNo) THEN
                                              EVALUATE(ItemNo,ClearTailSpace(COPYSTR(TempDocLine,16,14)));

                                            IF Item.GET(ItemNo) THEN
                                              SalesLine.VALIDATE("No.",ItemNo);
                                            //<TPZ2558>
                                            IF Item."Shortcut Dimension 5 Code" = 'P' THEN BEGIN
                                              SalesHeader.VALIDATE("Shortcut Dimension 5 Code",'P');
                                              SalesHeader.MODIFY;
                                            END;
                                            //</TPZ2558>

                                            //<TPZ1312>
                                            //EVALUATE(ExternalDocumentLineNo,COPYSTR(TempDocLine,11,3));
                                            ExternalDocumentLineNo := COPYSTR(TempDocLine,11,3);
                                            //</TPZ1312>
                                            SalesLine."External Document Line No." := ExternalDocumentLineNo;

                                            EVALUATE(UnitOfMeasure,ClearTailSpace(COPYSTR(TempDocLine,79,2)));

                                            EVALUATE(Description,ClearTailSpace(COPYSTR(TempDocLine,36,38)));
                                            SalesLine.Description := Description;
                                          END;
                                        '0252': ;
                                        '0253':
                                          BEGIN
                                            EVALUATE(QuantityOrdered,COPYSTR(TempDocLine,11,7));
                                            EVALUATE(QuantityShipped,COPYSTR(TempDocLine,19,7));
                                            EVALUATE(QuantityBackordered,COPYSTR(TempDocLine,27,7));
                                            EVALUATE(QuantityWhseBackordered,COPYSTR(TempDocLine,35,7));
                                            EVALUATE(UnitPrice,COPYSTR(TempDocLine,51,12));
                                            IF UnitOfMeasure = 'CM' THEN
                                              UnitPrice := UnitPrice / 100;

                                            IF (SalesLine.Type = SalesLine.Type::Item) AND
                                               (SalesLine."No." <> '')
                                            THEN BEGIN
                                              SalesLine.VALIDATE(Quantity,QuantityOrdered);
                                              SalesLine.VALIDATE("Qty. to Ship",QuantityShipped);

                                              IF SalesLine."Unit Price" <> 0 THEN
                                                Multiplier := UnitPrice / SalesLine."Unit Price"
                                              ELSE
                                                Multiplier := 1;

                                              SalesLine.VALIDATE("Actual Unit Price",UnitPrice);
                                              //<TPZ1125>
                                              // SalesLine."Unit Price Color":=SalesLine.SetStyle;
                                               SalesLine."Unit Price Color":= Table37EventSubscribers.Tb37_SetStyle(SalesLine); //TPZ2829 Event Conversion
                                              //</TPZ1125>
                                            END;

                                            SalesLine.MODIFY(TRUE);

                                            WhseReleaseLine.INIT;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Location Code" := SalesHeader."Location Code";
                                            WhseReleaseLine."File Name" := xFile.Name;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Batch Date" := BatchDate;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Batch Time" := BatchTime;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Release No." := ReleaseNo;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Customer No." := CustNo;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Order Date" := OrderDate;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."External Document No." := ExternalDocumentNo;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Shipping Agent and Service" := ShippingAgentAndService;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Shipping Payment Type" := ShippingPaymentType;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Backorder No." := BackorderNo;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Shipment Date" := ShipmentDate;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Freight Charge Amt." := FreightChargeAmt;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Ship-to Name" := SalesHeader."Ship-to Name";
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Ship-to Address" := SalesHeader."Ship-to Address";
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Ship-to Address 2" := SalesHeader."Ship-to Address 2";
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Ship-to City" := SalesHeader."Ship-to City";
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Ship-to County" := SalesHeader."Ship-to County";
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Ship-to Post Code" := SalesHeader."Ship-to Post Code";
                                            WhseReleaseLine."External Document Line No." := ExternalDocumentLineNo;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Item No." := ItemNo;
                                            WhseReleaseLine.Description := Description;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."UOM Code" := UnitOfMeasure;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Qty. Ordered" := QuantityOrdered;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Qty. Shipped" := QuantityShipped;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Qty. Backordered" := QuantityBackordered;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Qty. Whse. Backordered" := QuantityWhseBackordered;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Unit Price" := UnitPrice;
                                            WhseReleaseLine."Mfr. Rep. Code" := SalesHeader."Mfr. Rep. Code";

                                            IF WhseReleaseLine.INSERT THEN
                                              WhseReleaseLine.MODIFY;

                                            CommentLineCnt := 0;
                                            SalesCommentLine.RESET;
                                            SalesCommentLine.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesCommentLine."Document Type"::Order);
                                            SalesCommentLine.SETRANGE("No.",SalesHeader."No.");
                                            SalesCommentLine.SETRANGE("Document Line No.",0);
                                            IF SalesCommentLine.FIND('-') THEN
                                              REPEAT
                                                CASE CommentLineCnt OF
                                                  0: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL(Comment,SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  1: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 2",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  2: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 3",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  3: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 4",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  4: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 5",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  5: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 6",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  6: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 7",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  7: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 8",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  8: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 9",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  9: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 10",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  10: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 11",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  11: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 12",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  12: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 13",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  13: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 14",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  14: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 15",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  15: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 16",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  16: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 17",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  17: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 18",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  18: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 19",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                  19: WhseReleaseLine.MODIFYALL("Comment 20",SalesCommentLine.Comment);
                                                END;
                                                CommentLineCnt := CommentLineCnt + 1;
                                              UNTIL SalesCommentLine.NEXT = 0;
                                          END;
                                        '0254': ;
                                        '0290':
                                          BEGIN
                                            IF FreightChargeAmt <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                              SalesSetup.GET;
                                              SalesSetup.TESTFIELD(SalesSetup."Freight G/L Acc. No.");

                                              SalesLine2.RESET;
                                              SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document Type",SalesHeader."Document Type");
                                              SalesLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesHeader."No.");
                                              IF SalesLine2.FINDLAST THEN
                                                LineNo := SalesLine2."Line No." + 10000
                                              ELSE
                                                LineNo := 10000;

                                              SalesLine.INIT;
                                              SalesLine."Document Type" := SalesHeader."Document Type";
                                              SalesLine."Document No." := SalesHeader."No.";
                                              SalesLine."Line No." := LineNo;
                                              SalesLine.INSERT(TRUE);
                                              SalesLine."Sell-to Customer No." := SalesHeader."Sell-to Customer No.";
                                              SalesLine.VALIDATE(Type,SalesLine.Type::"G/L Account");
                                              SalesLine.VALIDATE("No.",SalesSetup."Freight G/L Acc. No.");
                                              SalesLine.VALIDATE(Quantity,1);
                                              SalesLine.VALIDATE("Unit Price",FreightChargeAmt);
                                              SalesLine.MODIFY(TRUE);
                                            END;
                                            COMMIT;
                                          END;
                                        '0299': ;
                                        '9999': ;
                                      END;
                                      TempDocLine := '';
                                      i := 0;
                                      WriteOK := FALSE;
                                    END;
                                  UNTIL j = 1;
                                  CommonInpFile.CLOSE;

                                  FILE.COPY(xFile.Path + xFile.Name,xFile.Path + 'Archive\' + xFile.Name);
                                  ERASE(xFile.Path + xFile.Name);
                                END;
                                 }

    PROCEDURE ClearTailSpace@1000000003(String@1000000000 : Text[80]) TextString : Text[80];
    VAR
      Xtmp@1000000002 : Text[80];
      i@1000000001 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      i := STRLEN(String);
      Xtmp := '';
      TextString := '';
      REPEAT
        Xtmp := COPYSTR(String,i,1);
        IF Xtmp = ' ' THEN
          i := i - 1;
      UNTIL (Xtmp <> ' ') OR (i=0);
      IF i = 0 THEN
        TextString := ''
      ELSE
        TextString := COPYSTR(String,1,i);
    END;

    PROCEDURE Trim@1000000000(String@1000000000 : Text[250]) : Text[250];
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELCHR(String,'<>',' '));
    END;

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
